NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

Notice is hereby given to the public that the members of the M/s. Atrium Medical India Private Limited having its
registered office at No.21, NP, Developed Plot, 1st Floor, Western Side, SIDCO Industrial Estate, Ekkaduthangal, Guindy,
Chennai, Tamil Nadu, India has passed special resolution at the Extra Ordinary General Meeting held on 25th March 2016
approving members Voluntarily winding-up and appointment of Liquidator.
“RESOLVED UNANIMOUSLY THAT pursuant to provisions of section 484 (1) (b) and other applicable provisions, if
any, of the Companies Act, 1956 and/or the Companies Act, 2013 as in force from time to time and in accordance with
the provisions of the Memorandum and Articles of Association of the Company and subject to the necessary approvals,
permissions and/or sanctions as may be necessary and required by any other appropriate authorities, institutions, or bodies,
if any, and subject to such other conditions and

modifications as may be prescribed by any of them in granting such

approvals, permissions and/or sanctions and having regard to the Declaration of Solvency made by the Board of Directors
at their meeting held on 23rd February 2016 and delivered to the Registrar of Companies Under section 488 (2) (a) of the
Companies Act, 1956 and/or the Companies Act, 2013 as in force from time to time stating that the company will be able
to pay its debts

in full and that the company will not be rendered insolvent within a period of three year from

the

commencement of the winding-up, the approval of share holders be and are hereby accorded for winding up of the company
and in this regard Mr.Prabhat Rastogi, Director of the company be and is hereby authorized under section 485(1) of the
Act,1956 and/or the Companies Act, 2013 as in force from time to time to give notice of the resolution by advertisement
in the Official Gazette, and also in two newspapers, one in English and one in Tamil circulating in Chennai within Fourteen
days from the date of this meeting.

RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provision of Section 490 (1) (a) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and/or the

as Liquidator of the company with a remuneration of Rs.10,000/- (Rupees Ten Thousand Only) for the purpose of winding
up of the affairs and to distribute the net realizable value of assets of the company after settlement of all creditors among
the share holders in proportion to their investment in the company and for conducting the entire process of winding-up and
exercise all such powers and discharge all such duties as stipulated in the provisions of the Companies Act.
